\subsection{Detailed Description}
Defines keyboard scancodes. 

\subsection{Enumeration Type Documentation}
\hypertarget{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777b}{\index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h}!S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Scancode@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Scancode}}
\index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Scancode@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Scancode}!SDL_scancode.h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Scancode}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}enum {\bf S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Scancode}}}\label{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777b}


The S\-D\-L keyboard scancode representation. 

Values of this type are used to represent keyboard keys, among other places in the \hyperlink{struct_s_d_l___keysym_ad47e9120a511e2efc7ec0c6d8a5ec51e}{key.\-keysym.\-scancode } field of the \hyperlink{union_s_d_l___event}{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-Event} structure.

The values in this enumeration are based on the U\-S\-B usage page standard\-: \href{http://www.usb.org/developers/devclass_docs/Hut1_12v2.pdf}{\tt http\-://www.\-usb.\-org/developers/devclass\-\_\-docs/\-Hut1\-\_\-12v2.\-pdf} \begin{Desc}

}]Located at the lower left of the return key on I\-S\-O keyboards and at the right end of the Q\-W\-E\-R\-T\-Y row on A\-N\-S\-I keyboards. Produces R\-E\-V\-E\-R\-S\-E S\-O\-L\-I\-D\-U\-S (backslash) and V\-E\-R\-T\-I\-C\-A\-L L\-I\-N\-E in a U\-S layout, R\-E\-V\-E\-R\-S\-E S\-O\-L\-I\-D\-U\-S and V\-E\-R\-T\-I\-C\-A\-L L\-I\-N\-E in a U\-K Mac layout, N\-U\-M\-B\-E\-R S\-I\-G\-N and T\-I\-L\-D\-E in a U\-K Windows layout, D\-O\-L\-L\-A\-R S\-I\-G\-N and P\-O\-U\-N\-D S\-I\-G\-N in a Swiss German layout, N\-U\-M\-B\-E\-R S\-I\-G\-N and A\-P\-O\-S\-T\-R\-O\-P\-H\-E in a German layout, G\-R\-A\-V\-E A\-C\-C\-E\-N\-T and P\-O\-U\-N\-D S\-I\-G\-N in a French Mac layout, and A\-S\-T\-E\-R\-I\-S\-K and M\-I\-C\-R\-O S\-I\-G\-N in a French Windows layout. \index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-U\-S\-H\-A\-S\-H@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-U\-S\-H\-A\-S\-H}!S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h}}\index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h}!S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-U\-S\-H\-A\-S\-H@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-U\-S\-H\-A\-S\-H}}\item[{\em 
\hypertarget{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777bac3a553bf8b10cc5fb62734c866e799e5}{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-U\-S\-H\-A\-S\-H}\label{_s_d_l__scancode_8h_a82ab7cff701034fb40a47b5b3a02777bac3a553bf8b10cc5fb62734c866e799e5}
}]I\-S\-O U\-S\-B keyboards actually use this code instead of 49 for the same key, but all O\-Ses I've seen treat the two codes identically. So, as an implementor, unless your keyboard generates both of those codes and your O\-S treats them differently, you should generate S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-B\-A\-C\-K\-S\-L\-A\-S\-H instead of this code. As a user, you should not rely on this code because S\-D\-L will never generate it with most (all?) keyboards. \index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-S\-E\-M\-I\-C\-O\-L\-O\-N@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-S\-E\-M\-I\-C\-O\-L\-O\-N}!S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h}}\index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h}!S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-S\-E\-M\-I\-C\-O\-L\-O\-N@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-S\-E\-M\-I\-C\-O\-L\-O\-N}}\item[{\em

}]\index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-A\-P\-O\-S\-T\-R\-O\-P\-H\-E@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-A\-P\-O\-S\-T\-R\-O\-P\-H\-E}!S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h}}\index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h}!S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-A\-P\-O\-S\-T\-R\-O\-P\-H\-E@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-A\-P\-O\-S\-T\-R\-O\-P\-H\-E}}\item[{\em

}]Located in the top left corner (on both A\-N\-S\-I and I\-S\-O keyboards). Produces G\-R\-A\-V\-E A\-C\-C\-E\-N\-T and T\-I\-L\-D\-E in a U\-S Windows layout and in U\-S and U\-K Mac layouts on A\-N\-S\-I keyboards, G\-R\-A\-V\-E A\-C\-C\-E\-N\-T and N\-O\-T S\-I\-G\-N in a U\-K Windows layout, S\-E\-C\-T\-I\-O\-N S\-I\-G\-N and P\-L\-U\-S-\/\-M\-I\-N\-U\-S S\-I\-G\-N in U\-S and U\-K Mac layouts on I\-S\-O keyboards, S\-E\-C\-T\-I\-O\-N S\-I\-G\-N and D\-E\-G\-R\-E\-E S\-I\-G\-N in a Swiss German layout (Mac\-: only on I\-S\-O keyboards), C\-I\-R\-C\-U\-M\-F\-L\-E\-X A\-C\-C\-E\-N\-T and D\-E\-G\-R\-E\-E S\-I\-G\-N in a German layout (Mac\-: only on I\-S\-O keyboards), S\-U\-P\-E\-R\-S\-C\-R\-I\-P\-T T\-W\-O and T\-I\-L\-D\-E in a French Windows layout, C\-O\-M\-M\-E\-R\-C\-I\-A\-L A\-T and N\-U\-M\-B\-E\-R S\-I\-G\-N in a French Mac layout on I\-S\-O keyboards, and L\-E\-S\-S-\/\-T\-H\-A\-N S\-I\-G\-N and G\-R\-E\-A\-T\-E\-R-\/\-T\-H\-A\-N S\-I\-G\-N in a Swiss German, German, or French Mac layout on A\-N\-S\-I keyboards. \index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-C\-O\-M\-M\-A@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-C\-O\-M\-M\-A}!S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h}}\index{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-scancode.\-h}!S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-C\-O\-M\-M\-A@{S\-D\-L\-\_\-\-S\-C\-A\-N\-C\-O\-D\-E\-\_\-\-C\-O\-M\-M\-A}}\item[{\em
